I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
MERGE should raise when multiple source rows match target row
# Environment

**Delta-rs version**: 0.16.4

**Binding**: Python 0.16.4

**Environment**:
- **Cloud provider**: None
- **OS**: MacOS Sonoma 14.4
- **Other**:

***
# Bug

**What happened**:
TableMerger.when_matched_update_all() inserts records when there is a match on multiple source columns
TableMerger.when_matched_update() inserts records when there is a match on multiple source columns


**What you expected to happen**:
TableMerger.when_matched_update_all() should throw an error if a target record matches multiple source records 
TableMerger.when_matched_update() should throw an error if a target record matches multiple source records 

They should never insert new records.

**How to reproduce it**:
Using polars 0.20.7
```python
import polars as pl
from deltalake import DeltaTable

base_df = pl.DataFrame(
    {
        "id": [1, 2],
        "attr": ["x", "y"]
    }
)

base_df.write_delta("./test_cdc", mode="overwrite")

dt = DeltaTable("./test_cdc")

print(pl.DataFrame(dt.to_pyarrow_table()))

cdc_df = pl.DataFrame(
    {
        "id": [1,1,1,2,2],
        "attr": ["a","b","c","d","e"],
        "op": ["U", "U", "U", "U", "U"]
    }
)


(
    dt.merge(
        cdc_df.to_arrow(),
        "s.id = t.id",
        source_alias="s",
        target_alias="t",
    )
    .when_matched_update(
        updates={"t.attr": "s.attr"},
        predicate="s.op = 'U'")
    .execute()
)

print(pl.DataFrame(dt.to_pyarrow_table()))
```

Gives the following output

**base table**
```bash
shape: (2, 2)
┌─────┬──────┐
│ id  ┆ attr │
│ --- ┆ ---  │
│ i64 ┆ str  │
╞═════╪══════╡
│ 1   ┆ x    │
│ 2   ┆ y    │
└─────┴──────┘
```

**After TableMerger is executed**
```bash
shape: (5, 2)
┌─────┬──────┐
│ id  ┆ attr │
│ --- ┆ ---  │
│ i64 ┆ str  │
╞═════╪══════╡
│ 2   ┆ d    │
│ 2   ┆ e    │
│ 1   ┆ a    │
│ 1   ┆ b    │
│ 1   ┆ c    │
└─────┴──────┘
```
**More details**:
Info on the specific case in slack: https://delta-users.slack.com/archives/C013LCAEB98/p1712673309723829

</pr_description>

   540	struct MergeOperationConfig {
   541	    /// Which records to update
   542	    predicate: Option<Expression>,
   543	    /// How to update columns in a record that match the predicate
   544	    operations: HashMap<Column, Expression>,
   545	    r#type: OperationType,
   546	}
   547	
   548	struct MergeOperation {
   549	    /// Which records to update
   550	    predicate: Option<Expr>,
   551	    /// How to update columns in a record that match the predicate
   552	    operations: HashMap<Column, Expr>,
   553	    r#type: OperationType,
   554	}
   555	
   556	impl MergeOperation {
   557	    fn try_from(
   558	        config: MergeOperationConfig,
   559	        schema: &DFSchema,
   560	        state: &dyn Session,
   561	        target_alias: &Option<String>,
   562	    ) -> DeltaResult<MergeOperation> {
   563	        let mut ops = HashMap::with_capacity(config.operations.capacity());
   564	
   565	        for (column, expression) in config.operations.into_iter() {
   566	            // Normalize the column name to contain the target alias. If a table reference was provided ensure it's the target.
   567	            let column = match target_alias {
   568	                Some(alias) => {
   569	                    let r = TableReference::bare(alias.to_owned());
   570	                    match column {
   571	                        Column {
   572	                            relation: None,
   573	                            name,
   574	                            spans,
   575	                        } => Column {
   576	                            relation: Some(r),
   577	                            name,
   578	                            spans,
   579	                        },
   580	                        Column {
   581	                            relation: Some(TableReference::Bare { table }),
   582	                            name,
   583	                            spans,
   584	                        } => {
   585	                            if table.as_ref() == alias {
   586	                                Column {
   587	                                    relation: Some(r),
   588	                                    name,
   589	                                    spans,
   590	                                }
   591	                            } else {
   592	                                return Err(DeltaTableError::Generic(format!(
   593	                                    "Table alias '{table}' in column reference '{table}.{name}' unknown. Hint: You must reference the Delta Table with alias '{alias}'."
   594	                                )));
   595	                            }
   596	                        }
   597	                        _ => {
   598	                            return Err(DeltaTableError::Generic(
   599	                                "Column must reference column in Delta table".into(),
   600	                            ));
   601	                        }
   602	                    }
   603	                }
   604	                None => column,
   605	            };
   606	            ops.insert(column, into_expr(expression, schema, state)?);
   607	        }
   608	
   609	        Ok(MergeOperation {
   610	            predicate: maybe_into_expr(config.predicate, schema, state)?,
   611	            operations: ops,
   612	            r#type: config.r#type,
   613	        })
   614	    }
   615	}

   671	impl ExtensionPlanner for MergeMetricExtensionPlanner {

   688	                            .add(batch.num_rows());
   689	                    },
   690	                )?));
   691	            }
   692	
   693	            if metric_observer.id.eq(TARGET_COUNT_ID) {
   694	                return Ok(Some(MetricObserverExec::try_new(
   695	                    TARGET_COUNT_ID.into(),
   696	                    physical_inputs,
   697	                    |batch, metrics| {
   698	                        MetricBuilder::new(metrics)
   699	                            .global_counter(TARGET_COUNT_METRIC)
   700	                            .add(batch.num_rows());
   701	                    },
   702	                )?));
   703	            }
   704	
   705	            if metric_observer.id.eq(OUTPUT_COUNT_ID) {
   706	                return Ok(Some(MetricObserverExec::try_new(
   707	                    OUTPUT_COUNT_ID.into(),
   708	                    physical_inputs,
   709	                    |batch, metrics| {
   710	                        MetricBuilder::new(metrics)
   711	                            .global_counter(TARGET_INSERTED_METRIC)
   712	                            .add(

   714	                                    .column_by_name(TARGET_INSERT_COLUMN)
   715	                                    .unwrap()
   716	                                    .null_count(),
   717	                            );
   718	                        MetricBuilder::new(metrics)
   719	                            .global_counter(TARGET_UPDATED_METRIC)
   720	                            .add(
   721	                                batch
   722	                                    .column_by_name(TARGET_UPDATE_COLUMN)
   723	                                    .unwrap()
   724	                                    .null_count(),
   725	                            );
   726	                        MetricBuilder::new(metrics)
   727	                            .global_counter(TARGET_DELETED_METRIC)
   728	                            .add(
   729	                                batch
   730	                                    .column_by_name(TARGET_DELETE_COLUMN)
   731	                                    .unwrap()
   732	                                    .null_count(),
   733	                            );
   734	                        MetricBuilder::new(metrics)

   739	                                    .unwrap()
   740	                                    .null_count(),
   741	                            );
   742	                    },
   743	                )?));
   744	            }
   745	        }
   746	
   747	        if let Some(barrier) = node.as_any().downcast_ref::<MergeBarrier>() {
   748	            if physical_inputs.len() != 1 {
   749	                return plan_err!("MergeBarrierExec expects exactly one input");
   750	            }
   751	            let schema = barrier.input.schema();

   764	#[tracing::instrument(skip_all, fields(operation = "merge", version = snapshot.version(), table_uri = %log_store.root_url()))]
   765	async fn execute(
   766	    predicate: Expression,
   767	    mut source: DataFrame,
   768	    log_store: LogStoreRef,
   769	    snapshot: EagerSnapshot,
   770	    state: SessionState,
   771	    writer_properties: Option<WriterProperties>,
   772	    mut commit_properties: CommitProperties,
   773	    _safe_cast: bool,
   774	    streaming: bool,
   775	    source_alias: Option<String>,
   776	    target_alias: Option<String>,
   777	    merge_schema: bool,
   778	    match_operations: Vec<MergeOperationConfig>,
   779	    not_match_target_operations: Vec<MergeOperationConfig>,
   780	    not_match_source_operations: Vec<MergeOperationConfig>,
   781	    operation_id: Uuid,
   782	    handle: Option<&Arc<dyn CustomExecuteHandler>>,
   783	) -> DeltaResult<(EagerSnapshot, MergeMetrics)> {
   784	    info!(
   785	        operation = "merge",
   786	        version = snapshot.version(),
   787	        "starting merge execution"
   788	    );
   789	
   790	    let mut metrics = MergeMetrics::default();
   791	    let exec_start = Instant::now();
   792	    // Determining whether we should write change data once so that computation of change data can
   793	    // be disabled in the common case(s)
   794	    let should_cdc = should_write_cdc(&snapshot)?;
   795	    // Change data may be collected and then written out at the completion of the merge
   796	
   797	    if should_cdc {
   798	        debug!("Executing a merge and I should write CDC!");
   799	    }
   800	
   801	    info!(cdc_enabled = should_cdc, "merge execution details");
   802	
   803	    let current_metadata = snapshot.metadata();
   804	    let merge_planner = DeltaPlanner::new();
   805	
   806	    let state = SessionStateBuilder::new_from_existing(state)
   807	        .with_query_planner(merge_planner)
   808	        .build();
   809	
   810	    // TODO: Given the join predicate, remove any expression that involve the
   811	    // source table and keep expressions that only involve the target table.
   812	    // This would allow us to perform statistics/partition pruning E.G
   813	    // Expression source.id = id and to_dt = '9999-12-31' -Becomes-> to_dt =
   814	    // '9999-12-31'
   815	    //
   816	    // If the user specified any not_source_match operations then those
   817	    // predicates also need to be considered when pruning
   818	
   819	    let source_name = match &source_alias {
   820	        Some(alias) => TableReference::bare(alias.to_string()),
   821	        None => TableReference::bare(UNNAMED_TABLE),
   822	    };
   823	
   824	    let target_name = match &target_alias {
   825	        Some(alias) => TableReference::bare(alias.to_string()),
   826	        None => TableReference::bare(UNNAMED_TABLE),
   827	    };
   828	
   829	    let mut generated_col_exp = None;
   830	    let mut missing_generated_col = None;
   831	
   832	    if gc_is_enabled(&snapshot) {
   833	        let generated_col_expressions = snapshot.schema().get_generated_columns()?;
   834	        let (source_with_gc, missing_generated_columns) =
   835	            add_missing_generated_columns(source, &generated_col_expressions)?;
   836	
   837	        source = source_with_gc;
   838	        generated_col_exp = Some(generated_col_expressions);
   839	        missing_generated_col = Some(missing_generated_columns);
   840	    }
   841	    // This is only done to provide the source columns with a correct table reference. Just renaming the columns does not work
   842	    let source = LogicalPlanBuilder::scan(
   843	        source_name.clone(),
   844	        provider_as_source(source.into_view()),
   845	        None,
   846	    )?
   847	    .build()?;
   848	
   849	    let source = LogicalPlan::Extension(Extension {
   850	        node: Arc::new(MetricObserver {
   851	            id: SOURCE_COUNT_ID.into(),
   852	            input: source,
   853	            enable_pushdown: false,
   854	        }),
   855	    });
   856	
   857	    let file_column = Arc::new(resolve_file_column_name(
   858	        snapshot.input_schema().as_ref(),
   859	        None,
   860	    )?);
   861	
   862	    let target_provider = provider_as_source(
   863	        DeltaScanNext::builder()
   864	            .with_eager_snapshot(snapshot.clone())
   865	            .with_log_store(log_store.clone())
   866	            .with_file_column(file_column.as_str())
   867	            .await?,
   868	    );
   869	    let target =
   870	        LogicalPlanBuilder::scan(target_name.clone(), target_provider.clone(), None)?.build()?;
   871	
   872	    let source_schema = source.schema();
   873	    let target_schema = target.schema();
   874	
   875	    let join_schema_df = build_join_schema(source_schema, target_schema, &JoinType::Full)?;
   876	
   877	    let predicate = predicate.resolve(&state, Arc::new(join_schema_df.clone()))?;
   878	
   879	    // Attempt to construct an early filter that we can apply to the Add action list and the delta scan.
   880	    // In the case where there are partition columns in the join predicate, we can scan the source table
   881	    // to get the distinct list of partitions affected and constrain the search to those.
   882	
   883	    let target_subset_filter: Option<Expr> = if !not_match_source_operations.is_empty() {
   884	        // It's only worth trying to create an early filter where there are no `when_not_matched_source` operators, since
   885	        // that implies a full scan
   886	        None
   887	    } else {
   888	        try_construct_early_filter(
   889	            predicate.clone(),
   890	            &snapshot,
   891	            &state,
   892	            &source,
   893	            &source_name,
   894	            &target_name,
   895	            streaming,
   896	        )
   897	        .await?
   898	    }
   899	    .map(|e| normalize_target_subset_filter(target.schema().clone(), e))
   900	    .transpose()?;

   947	    });

   949	    let target = target.with_column(TARGET_COLUMN, lit(true))?;
   950	
   951	    let join = source.join(target, JoinType::Full, &[], &[], Some(predicate.clone()))?;
   952	    let join_schema_df = join.schema().to_owned();
   953	
   954	    let match_operations: Vec<MergeOperation> = match_operations
   955	        .into_iter()
   956	        .map(|op| MergeOperation::try_from(op, &join_schema_df, &state, &target_alias))
   957	        .collect::<Result<Vec<MergeOperation>, DeltaTableError>>()?;
   958	
   959	    let not_match_target_operations: Vec<MergeOperation> = not_match_target_operations
   960	        .into_iter()
   961	        .map(|op| MergeOperation::try_from(op, &join_schema_df, &state, &target_alias))
   962	        .collect::<Result<Vec<MergeOperation>, DeltaTableError>>()?;
   963	
   964	    let not_match_source_operations: Vec<MergeOperation> = not_match_source_operations
   965	        .into_iter()
   966	        .map(|op| MergeOperation::try_from(op, &join_schema_df, &state, &target_alias))
   967	        .collect::<Result<Vec<MergeOperation>, DeltaTableError>>()?;
   968	
   969	    // merge_arrow_schema is used to tell whether the two schema can be merge but we use the operation statement to pick new columns
   970	    // this avoid the side effect of adding unnecessary columns (eg. target.id = source.ID) "ID" will not be added since "id" exist in target and end user intended it to be "id"
   971	    let mut new_schema = None;
   972	    let mut schema_action = None;
   973	    if merge_schema {
   974	        let logical_schema = snapshot.input_schema();
   975	        // Use the table schema here. Scan-time encodings for partition columns should not
   976	        // affect schema evolution.
   977	        let logical_target_schema =
   978	            DFSchema::try_from_qualified_schema(target_name.clone(), logical_schema.as_ref())?;
   979	        let merge_schema =
   980	            merge_arrow_schema(logical_schema, source_schema.inner().clone(), false)?;
   981	
   982	        let mut schema_builder = SchemaBuilder::from(merge_schema.deref());
   983	
   984	        modify_schema(
   985	            &mut schema_builder,
   986	            &logical_target_schema,
   987	            source_schema,
   988	            &match_operations,
   989	        )?;
   990	
   991	        modify_schema(
   992	            &mut schema_builder,
   993	            &logical_target_schema,
   994	            source_schema,
   995	            &not_match_source_operations,
   996	        )?;
   997	
   998	        modify_schema(
   999	            &mut schema_builder,
  1000	            &logical_target_schema,
  1001	            source_schema,
  1002	            &not_match_target_operations,
  1003	        )?;
  1004	        let schema = Arc::new(schema_builder.finish());
  1005	        new_schema = Some(schema.clone());
  1006	        let schema_struct: StructType = schema.try_into_kernel()?;
  1007	        if &schema_struct != snapshot.schema().as_ref() {
  1008	            let action = Action::Metadata(new_metadata(
  1009	                &schema_struct,
  1010	                current_metadata.partition_columns(),
  1011	                snapshot.metadata().configuration(),
  1012	            )?);
  1013	            schema_action = Some(action);
  1014	        }
  1015	    }
  1016	
  1017	    let matched = col(SOURCE_COLUMN)
  1018	        .is_true()
  1019	        .and(col(TARGET_COLUMN).is_true());
  1020	    let not_matched_target = col(SOURCE_COLUMN)
  1021	        .is_true()
  1022	        .and(col(TARGET_COLUMN).is_null());
  1023	    let not_matched_source = col(SOURCE_COLUMN)
  1024	        .is_null()
  1025	        .and(col(TARGET_COLUMN))
  1026	        .is_true();
  1027	
  1028	    // Plus 3 for the default operations for each match category
  1029	    let operations_size = match_operations.len()
  1030	        + not_match_source_operations.len()
  1031	        + not_match_target_operations.len()
  1032	        + 3;
  1033	
  1034	    let mut when_expr = Vec::with_capacity(operations_size);
  1035	    let mut then_expr = Vec::with_capacity(operations_size);
  1036	    let mut ops = Vec::with_capacity(operations_size);
  1037	
  1038	    fn update_case(
  1039	        operations: Vec<MergeOperation>,
  1040	        ops: &mut Vec<(HashMap<Column, Expr>, OperationType)>,
  1041	        when_expr: &mut Vec<Expr>,
  1042	        then_expr: &mut Vec<Expr>,
  1043	        base_expr: &Expr,
  1044	    ) -> DeltaResult<Vec<MergePredicate>> {
  1045	        let mut predicates = Vec::with_capacity(operations.len());
  1046	
  1047	        for op in operations {
  1048	            let predicate = match &op.predicate {
  1049	                Some(predicate) => base_expr.clone().and(predicate.to_owned()),
  1050	                None => base_expr.clone(),
  1051	            };
  1052	
  1053	            when_expr.push(predicate);
  1054	            then_expr.push(lit(ops.len() as i32));
  1055	
  1056	            ops.push((op.operations, op.r#type));
  1057	
  1058	            let action_type = match op.r#type {
  1059	                OperationType::Update => "update",
  1060	                OperationType::Delete => "delete",
  1061	                OperationType::Insert => "insert",
  1062	                OperationType::SourceDelete => {
  1063	                    return Err(DeltaTableError::Generic("Invalid action type".to_string()));
  1064	                }
  1065	                OperationType::Copy => {
  1066	                    return Err(DeltaTableError::Generic("Invalid action type".to_string()));
  1067	                }
  1068	            };
  1069	
  1070	            let action_type = action_type.to_string();
  1071	            let predicate = op
  1072	                .predicate
  1073	                .map(|expr| fmt_expr_to_sql(&expr))
  1074	                .transpose()?;
  1075	
  1076	            predicates.push(MergePredicate {
  1077	                action_type,
  1078	                predicate,
  1079	            });
  1080	        }
  1081	        Ok(predicates)
  1082	    }
  1083	
  1084	    let match_operations = update_case(
  1085	        match_operations,
  1086	        &mut ops,
  1087	        &mut when_expr,
  1088	        &mut then_expr,
  1089	        &matched,
  1090	    )?;
  1091	
  1092	    let not_match_target_operations = update_case(
  1093	        not_match_target_operations,
  1094	        &mut ops,
  1095	        &mut when_expr,
  1096	        &mut then_expr,
  1097	        &not_matched_target,
  1098	    )?;
  1099	
  1100	    let not_match_source_operations = update_case(
  1101	        not_match_source_operations,
  1102	        &mut ops,
  1103	        &mut when_expr,
  1104	        &mut then_expr,
  1105	        &not_matched_source,
  1106	    )?;
  1107	
  1108	    when_expr.push(matched);
  1109	    then_expr.push(lit(ops.len() as i32));
  1110	    ops.push((HashMap::new(), OperationType::Copy));
  1111	
  1112	    when_expr.push(not_matched_target);
  1113	    then_expr.push(lit(ops.len() as i32));
  1114	    ops.push((HashMap::new(), OperationType::SourceDelete));
  1115	
  1116	    when_expr.push(not_matched_source);
  1117	    then_expr.push(lit(ops.len() as i32));
  1118	    ops.push((HashMap::new(), OperationType::Copy));
  1119	
  1120	    let case = CaseBuilder::new(None, when_expr, then_expr, None).end()?;
  1121	
  1122	    let projection = join.with_column(OPERATION_COLUMN, case)?;
  1123	
  1124	    let mut new_columns = vec![];
  1125	
  1126	    let mut write_projection = Vec::new();
  1127	    let mut write_projection_with_cdf = Vec::new();
  1128	
  1129	    let schema = if let Some(schema) = new_schema {
  1130	        Arc::new(schema.try_into_kernel()?)
  1131	    } else {
  1132	        snapshot.schema()
  1133	    };
  1134	
  1135	    for delta_field in schema.fields() {
  1136	        let mut when_expr = Vec::with_capacity(operations_size);
  1137	        let mut then_expr = Vec::with_capacity(operations_size);
  1138	
  1139	        let qualifier = match &target_alias {
  1140	            Some(alias) => Some(TableReference::Bare {
  1141	                table: alias.to_owned().into(),
  1142	            }),
  1143	            None => TableReference::none(),
  1144	        };
  1145	        let mut null_target_column = None;
  1146	
  1147	        let source_qualifier = match &source_alias {
  1148	            Some(alias) => Some(TableReference::Bare {
  1149	                table: alias.to_owned().into(),
  1150	            }),
  1151	            None => TableReference::none(),
  1152	        };
  1153	        let name = delta_field.name();
  1154	        let mut cast_type: DataType = delta_field.data_type().try_into_arrow()?;
  1155	
  1156	        // Receive the correct column reference given that some columns are only in source table
  1157	        let column = if let Some(field) = snapshot.schema().field(name) {
  1158	            if field == delta_field {
  1159	                Column::new(qualifier.clone(), name)
  1160	            } else {
  1161	                // when there is a change in the field such as an added column in a nested data types casts will break with the new field data type
  1162	                let col_ref = Column::new(source_qualifier.clone(), name);
  1163	                cast_type = source_schema.data_type(&col_ref)?.to_owned();
  1164	                col_ref
  1165	            }
  1166	        } else {
  1167	            null_target_column = Some(cast(
  1168	                lit(ScalarValue::Null).alias(name),
  1169	                delta_field.data_type().try_into_arrow()?,
  1170	            ));
  1171	            Column::new(source_qualifier.clone(), name)
  1172	        };
  1173	
  1174	        for (idx, (operations, _)) in ops.iter().enumerate() {
  1175	            let op = operations
  1176	                .get(&column)
  1177	                .map(|expr| expr.to_owned())
  1178	                .unwrap_or_else(|| col(column.clone()));
  1179	
  1180	            when_expr.push(lit(idx as i32));
  1181	            then_expr.push(op);
  1182	        }
  1183	
  1184	        let case = CaseBuilder::new(
  1185	            Some(Box::new(col(OPERATION_COLUMN))),
  1186	            when_expr,
  1187	            then_expr,
  1188	            None,
  1189	        )
  1190	        .end()?;
  1191	
  1192	        let name = "__delta_rs_c_".to_owned() + delta_field.name();
  1193	
  1194	        write_projection.push(cast(
  1195	            Expr::Column(Column::from_name(name.clone())).alias(delta_field.name()),
  1196	            cast_type.clone(),
  1197	        ));
  1198	
  1199	        write_projection_with_cdf.push(
  1200	            when(
  1201	                col(CDC_COLUMN_NAME).not_eq(lit("update_preimage")),
  1202	                cast(
  1203	                    Expr::Column(Column::from_name(name.clone())),
  1204	                    cast_type.clone(),
  1205	                ),
  1206	            )
  1207	            .otherwise(null_target_column.unwrap_or(cast(
  1208	                Expr::Column(Column::new(qualifier, delta_field.name())),
  1209	                cast_type,
  1210	            )))? // We take the column from target table but in case of schema evolution we assign the column as null
  1211	            .alias(delta_field.name()),
  1212	        );
  1213	        new_columns.push((name, case));
  1214	    }
  1215	
  1216	    write_projection_with_cdf.push(col("_change_type"));
  1217	
  1218	    let mut insert_when = Vec::with_capacity(ops.len());
  1219	    let mut insert_then = Vec::with_capacity(ops.len());
  1220	
  1221	    let mut update_when = Vec::with_capacity(ops.len());
  1222	    let mut update_then = Vec::with_capacity(ops.len());
  1223	
  1224	    let mut target_delete_when = Vec::with_capacity(ops.len());
  1225	    let mut target_delete_then = Vec::with_capacity(ops.len());
  1226	
  1227	    let mut delete_when = Vec::with_capacity(ops.len());
  1228	    let mut delete_then = Vec::with_capacity(ops.len());
  1229	
  1230	    let mut copy_when = Vec::with_capacity(ops.len());
  1231	    let mut copy_then = Vec::with_capacity(ops.len());
  1232	
  1233	    for (idx, (_operations, r#type)) in ops.iter().enumerate() {
  1234	        let op = idx as i32;
  1235	
  1236	        // Used to indicate the record should be dropped prior to write
  1237	        delete_when.push(lit(op));
  1238	        delete_then.push(lit(matches!(
  1239	            r#type,
  1240	            OperationType::Delete | OperationType::SourceDelete
  1241	        )));
  1242	
  1243	        // Use the null count on these arrays to determine how many records satisfy the predicate
  1244	        insert_when.push(lit(op));
  1245	        insert_then.push(
  1246	            when(
  1247	                lit(matches!(r#type, OperationType::Insert)),
  1248	                lit(ScalarValue::Boolean(None)),
  1249	            )
  1250	            .otherwise(lit(false))?,
  1251	        );
  1252	
  1253	        update_when.push(lit(op));
  1254	        update_then.push(
  1255	            when(
  1256	                lit(matches!(r#type, OperationType::Update)),
  1257	                lit(ScalarValue::Boolean(None)),
  1258	            )
  1259	            .otherwise(lit(false))?,
  1260	        );
  1261	
  1262	        target_delete_when.push(lit(op));
  1263	        target_delete_then.push(
  1264	            when(
  1265	                lit(matches!(r#type, OperationType::Delete)),
  1266	                lit(ScalarValue::Boolean(None)),
  1267	            )
  1268	            .otherwise(lit(false))?,
  1269	        );
  1270	
  1271	        copy_when.push(lit(op));
  1272	        copy_then.push(
  1273	            when(
  1274	                lit(matches!(r#type, OperationType::Copy)),
  1275	                lit(ScalarValue::Boolean(None)),
  1276	            )
  1277	            .otherwise(lit(false))?,
  1278	        );
  1279	    }
  1280	
  1281	    fn build_case(when: Vec<Expr>, then: Vec<Expr>) -> DataFusionResult<Expr> {
  1282	        CaseBuilder::new(
  1283	            Some(Box::new(col(OPERATION_COLUMN))),
  1284	            when,
  1285	            then,
  1286	            Some(Box::new(lit(false))),
  1287	        )
  1288	        .end()
  1289	    }
  1290	
  1291	    new_columns.push((
  1292	        DELETE_COLUMN.to_owned(),
  1293	        build_case(delete_when, delete_then)?,
  1294	    ));
  1295	    new_columns.push((
  1296	        TARGET_INSERT_COLUMN.to_owned(),
  1297	        build_case(insert_when, insert_then)?,
  1298	    ));
  1299	    new_columns.push((
  1300	        TARGET_UPDATE_COLUMN.to_owned(),
  1301	        build_case(update_when, update_then)?,
  1302	    ));
  1303	    new_columns.push((
  1304	        TARGET_DELETE_COLUMN.to_owned(),
  1305	        build_case(target_delete_when, target_delete_then)?,
  1306	    ));
  1307	    new_columns.push((
  1308	        TARGET_COPY_COLUMN.to_owned(),
  1309	        build_case(copy_when, copy_then)?,
  1310	    ));
  1311	
  1312	    let new_columns = {
  1313	        let plan = projection.into_unoptimized_plan();
  1314	        let mut fields: Vec<Expr> = plan
  1315	            .schema()
  1316	            .columns()
  1317	            .iter()
  1318	            .map(|f| col(f.clone()))
  1319	            .collect();
  1320	
  1321	        fields.extend(new_columns.into_iter().map(|(name, ex)| ex.alias(name)));
  1322	
  1323	        LogicalPlanBuilder::from(plan).project(fields)?.build()?
  1324	    };
  1325	
  1326	    let distribute_expr = col(file_column.as_str());
  1327	
  1328	    let merge_barrier = LogicalPlan::Extension(Extension {
  1329	        node: Arc::new(MergeBarrier {
  1330	            input: new_columns.clone(),
  1331	            expr: distribute_expr,
  1332	            file_column: Arc::clone(&file_column),
  1333	        }),
  1334	    });
  1335	
  1336	    // We should observe the metrics before we union the merge plan with the cdf_merge plan
  1337	    // so that we get the metrics only for the merge plan.
  1338	    let operation_count = LogicalPlan::Extension(Extension {
  1339	        node: Arc::new(MetricObserver {
  1340	            id: OUTPUT_COUNT_ID.into(),
  1341	            input: merge_barrier,
  1342	            enable_pushdown: false,
  1343	        }),
  1344	    });
  1345	
  1346	    let operation_count = DataFrame::new(state.clone(), operation_count);
  1347	
  1348	    let mut projected = if should_cdc {
  1349	        operation_count
  1350	            .clone()

  1412	
  1413	    // Prefer target-branch scan metrics.
  1414	    let scan_count = find_node::<DeltaScanExec>(&target_count)
  1415	        .or_else(|| find_node::<DeltaScanExec>(&write))
  1416	        .ok_or_else(err)?;
  1417	
  1418	    let table_partition_cols = current_metadata.partition_columns().clone();
  1419	    let writer_stats_config = WriterStatsConfig::from_config(snapshot.table_configuration());
  1420	
  1421	    let (mut actions, write_plan_metrics) = write_execution_plan_v2(
  1422	        Some(&snapshot),
  1423	        &state,
  1424	        write,
  1425	        table_partition_cols.clone(),
  1426	        log_store.object_store(Some(operation_id)),
  1427	        Some(snapshot.table_properties().target_file_size()),
  1428	        None,
  1429	        writer_properties.clone(),
  1430	        writer_stats_config.clone(),
  1431	        None,
  1432	        should_cdc, // if true, write execution plan splits batches in [normal, cdc] data before writing
  1433	    )
  1434	    .await?;
  1435	    if let Some(schema_metadata) = schema_action {
  1436	        actions.push(schema_metadata);
  1437	    }
  1438	
  1439	    metrics.rewrite_time_ms = write_plan_metrics.write_time_ms;
  1440	    metrics.scan_time_ms = write_plan_metrics.scan_time_ms;
  1441	    metrics.num_target_files_added = actions.len();
  1442	
  1443	    let survivors = barrier
  1444	        .as_any()
  1445	        .downcast_ref::<MergeBarrierExec>()
  1446	        .unwrap()
  1447	        .survivors();
  1448	
  1449	    let table_root = snapshot.table_configuration().table_root().clone();
  1450	
  1451	    for action in snapshot.log_data() {
  1452	        let rel_path = action.path();
  1453	        let rel_path_str = rel_path.as_ref();
  1454	
  1455	        if should_remove_rewritten_file(&survivors, rel_path_str, &table_root)? {
  1456	            metrics.num_target_files_removed += 1;
  1457	            actions.push(action.remove_action(true).into());
  1458	        }
  1459	    }
  1460	
  1461	    let source_count_metrics = source_count.metrics().unwrap();
  1462	    let target_count_metrics = op_count.metrics().unwrap();
  1463	    let scan_count_metrics = scan_count.metrics().unwrap();
  1464	
  1465	    metrics.num_source_rows = get_metric(&source_count_metrics, SOURCE_COUNT_METRIC);
  1466	    metrics.num_target_rows_inserted = get_metric(&target_count_metrics, TARGET_INSERTED_METRIC);
  1467	    metrics.num_target_rows_updated = get_metric(&target_count_metrics, TARGET_UPDATED_METRIC);
  1468	    metrics.num_target_rows_deleted = get_metric(&target_count_metrics, TARGET_DELETED_METRIC);
  1469	    metrics.num_target_rows_copied = get_metric(&target_count_metrics, TARGET_COPY_METRIC);
  1470	    metrics.num_output_rows = metrics.num_target_rows_inserted
  1471	        + metrics.num_target_rows_updated
  1472	        + metrics.num_target_rows_copied;
  1473	    let target_files_scanned_metric_names = [
  1474	        TARGET_FILES_SCANNED_METRIC,
  1475	        TARGET_FILES_SCANNED_METRIC_LEGACY,
  1476	    ];
  1477	    metrics.num_target_files_scanned = get_metric_any_or(
  1478	        &scan_count_metrics,
  1479	        &target_files_scanned_metric_names,
  1480	        || {
  1481	            warn!(
  1482	                %operation_id,
  1483	                metric_names = ?target_files_scanned_metric_names,
  1484	                "Missing target scan metric; defaulting target files scanned to zero"
  1485	            );
  1486	            0
  1487	        },
  1488	    );
  1489	
  1490	    let target_files_skipped_metric_names = [
  1491	        TARGET_FILES_PRUNED_METRIC,
  1492	        TARGET_FILES_SKIPPED_METRIC,
  1493	        TARGET_FILES_PRUNED_METRIC_LEGACY,
  1494	    ];
  1495	    metrics.num_target_files_skipped_during_scan = get_metric_any_or(
  1496	        &scan_count_metrics,
  1497	        &target_files_skipped_metric_names,
  1498	        || {
  1499	            let total_files = snapshot.log_data().num_files();
  1500	            let (derived, impossible_state) =
  1501	                derive_skipped_file_count(total_files, metrics.num_target_files_scanned);
  1502	            if impossible_state {
  1503	                warn!(
  1504	                    %operation_id,
  1505	                    total_files,
  1506	                    scanned_files = metrics.num_target_files_scanned,
  1507	                    metric_names = ?target_files_skipped_metric_names,
  1508	                    "Target scan metrics reported more scanned files than exist; clamping derived skipped-file count to zero"
  1509	                );
  1510	            }
  1511	            warn!(
  1512	                %operation_id,
  1513	                metric_names = ?target_files_skipped_metric_names,
  1514	                derived,
  1515	                "Missing target skipped-file metric; deriving from total-files minus scanned-files"
  1516	            );
  1517	            derived
  1518	        },
  1519	    );
  1520	    metrics.execution_time_ms = Instant::now().duration_since(exec_start).as_millis() as u64;
  1521	
  1522	    let app_metadata = &mut commit_properties.app_metadata;
  1523	    app_metadata.insert("readVersion".to_owned(), snapshot.version().into());
  1524	    if let Ok(map) = serde_json::to_value(&metrics) {
  1525	        app_metadata.insert("operationMetrics".to_owned(), map);
  1526	    }
  1527	
  1528	    // Do not make a commit when there are zero updates to the state
  1529	    let operation = DeltaOperation::Merge {
  1530	        predicate: commit_predicate,
  1531	        merge_predicate: Some(fmt_expr_to_sql(&predicate)?),
  1532	        matched_predicates: match_operations,
  1533	        not_matched_predicates: not_match_target_operations,
  1534	        not_matched_by_source_predicates: not_match_source_operations,
  1535	    };
  1536	
  1537	    if actions.is_empty() {
  1538	        return Ok((snapshot, metrics));
  1539	    }
  1540	
  1541	    let commit = CommitBuilder::from(commit_properties)
  1542	        .with_actions(actions)
  1543	        .with_operation_id(operation_id)
  1544	        .with_post_commit_hook_handler(handle.cloned())
  1545	        .build(Some(&snapshot), log_store.clone(), operation)
  1546	        .await?;
  1547	    Ok((commit.snapshot().snapshot, metrics))
  1548	}
  1549	
  1550	fn modify_schema(
  1551	    ending_schema: &mut SchemaBuilder,
  1552	    target_schema: &DFSchema,
  1553	    source_schema: &DFSchema,
  1554	    operations: &[MergeOperation],
  1555	) -> DeltaResult<()> {
  1556	    for columns in operations
  1557	        .iter()
  1558	        .filter(|ops| matches!(ops.r#type, OperationType::Update | OperationType::Insert))
  1559	        .flat_map(|ops| ops.operations.keys())
  1560	    {

     2	//! predicate.  A full outer join is performed which results in source and
     3	//! target records that match, source records that do not match, or target
     4	//! records that do not match.
     5	//!
     6	//! Users can specify update, delete, and insert operations for these categories
     7	//! and specify additional predicates for finer control. The order of operations
     8	//! specified matter.  See [`MergeBuilder`] for more information
     9	//!
    10	//! # Example
    11	//! ```rust ignore
    12	//! let table = open_table(Url::from_directory_path("/abs/path/to/table").unwrap())?;

    28	//!     .await?

//! Merge Barrier determines which files have modifications during the merge operation
//!
//! For every unique path in the input stream, a barrier is established. If any
//! single record for a file contains any delete, update, or insert operations
//! then the barrier for the file is opened and can be sent downstream.
//! To determine if a file contains zero changes, the input stream is
//! exhausted. Afterwards, records are then dropped.
//!
//! Bookkeeping is maintained to determine which files have modifications, so
//! they can be removed from the delta log.

use std::{
    collections::HashMap,
    pin::Pin,
    sync::Arc,
    task::{Context, Poll},
};

use arrow::array::{Array, ArrayRef, RecordBatch, builder::UInt64Builder};
use arrow::datatypes::SchemaRef;
use dashmap::DashSet;
use datafusion::common::{DataFusionError, Result as DataFusionResult};
use datafusion::logical_expr::{Expr, LogicalPlan, UserDefinedLogicalNodeCore};
use datafusion::physical_expr::{Distribution, PhysicalExpr};
use datafusion::physical_plan::{
    DisplayAs, DisplayFormatType, ExecutionPlan, RecordBatchStream, SendableRecordBatchStream,
};
use futures::{Stream, StreamExt};

use crate::{
    DeltaTableError,
    delta_datafusion::get_path_column,
    operations::merge::{TARGET_DELETE_COLUMN, TARGET_INSERT_COLUMN, TARGET_UPDATE_COLUMN},
};

pub(crate) type BarrierSurvivorSet = Arc<DashSet<String>>;

#[derive(Debug)]
/// Physical Node for the MergeBarrier
/// Batches to this node must be repartitioned on col('deleta_rs_path').
/// Each record batch then undergoes further partitioning based on the file column to it's corresponding barrier
pub struct MergeBarrierExec {
    input: Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>,
    file_column: Arc<String>,
    survivors: BarrierSurvivorSet,
    expr: Arc<dyn PhysicalExpr>,
}

impl MergeBarrierExec {
    /// Create a new MergeBarrierExec Node
    pub fn new(
        input: Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>,
        file_column: Arc<String>,
        expr: Arc<dyn PhysicalExpr>,
    ) -> Self {
        MergeBarrierExec {
            input,
            file_column,
            survivors: Arc::new(DashSet::new()),
            expr,
        }
    }

    /// Files that have modifications to them and need to removed from the delta log
    pub fn survivors(&self) -> BarrierSurvivorSet {
        self.survivors.clone()
    }
}

impl ExecutionPlan for MergeBarrierExec {
    fn name(&self) -> &str {
        Self::static_name()
    }

    fn as_any(&self) -> &dyn std::any::Any {
        self
    }

    fn schema(&self) -> arrow_schema::SchemaRef {
        self.input.schema()
    }

    fn properties(&self) -> &datafusion::physical_plan::PlanProperties {
        self.input.properties()
    }

    fn required_input_distribution(&self) -> Vec<Distribution> {
        vec![Distribution::HashPartitioned(vec![self.expr.clone()]); 1]
    }

    fn children(&self) -> Vec<&Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>> {
        vec![&self.input]
    }

    fn with_new_children(
        self: Arc<Self>,
        children: Vec<Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>>,
    ) -> datafusion::common::Result<Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>> {
        if children.len() != 1 {
            return Err(DataFusionError::Plan(
                "MergeBarrierExec wrong number of children".to_string(),
            ));
        }
        Ok(Arc::new(MergeBarrierExec::new(
            children[0].clone(),
            self.file_column.clone(),
            self.expr.clone(),
        )))
    }

    fn execute(
        &self,
        partition: usize,
        context: Arc<datafusion::execution::TaskContext>,
    ) -> datafusion::common::Result<datafusion::physical_plan::SendableRecordBatchStream> {
        let input = self.input.execute(partition, context)?;
        Ok(Box::pin(MergeBarrierStream::new(
            input,
            self.schema(),
            self.survivors.clone(),
            self.file_column.clone(),
        )))
    }
}

impl DisplayAs for MergeBarrierExec {
    fn fmt_as(&self, t: DisplayFormatType, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter) -> std::fmt::Result {
        match t {
            DisplayFormatType::Default
            | DisplayFormatType::Verbose
            | DisplayFormatType::TreeRender => {
                write!(f, "MergeBarrier",)?;
                Ok(())
            }
        }
    }
}

#[derive(Debug)]
enum State {
    Feed,
    Drain,
    Finalize,
    Abort,
    Done,
}

#[derive(Debug)]
enum PartitionBarrierState {
    Closed,
    Open,
}

#[derive(Debug)]
struct MergeBarrierPartition {
    state: PartitionBarrierState,
    buffer: Vec<RecordBatch>,
    file_name: Option<String>,
}

impl MergeBarrierPartition {
    pub fn new(file_name: Option<String>) -> Self {
        MergeBarrierPartition {
            state: PartitionBarrierState::Closed,
            buffer: Vec::new(),
            file_name,
        }
    }

    pub fn feed(&mut self, batch: RecordBatch) -> DataFusionResult<()> {
        match self.state {
            PartitionBarrierState::Closed => {
                let delete_count = get_count(&batch, TARGET_DELETE_COLUMN)?;
                let update_count = get_count(&batch, TARGET_UPDATE_COLUMN)?;
                let insert_count = get_count(&batch, TARGET_INSERT_COLUMN)?;
                self.buffer.push(batch);

                if insert_count > 0 || update_count > 0 || delete_count > 0 {
                    self.state = PartitionBarrierState::Open;
                }
            }
            PartitionBarrierState::Open => {
                self.buffer.push(batch);
            }
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    pub fn drain(&mut self) -> Option<RecordBatch> {
        match self.state {
            PartitionBarrierState::Closed => None,
            PartitionBarrierState::Open => self.buffer.pop(),
        }
    }
}

struct MergeBarrierStream {
    schema: SchemaRef,
    state: State,
    input: SendableRecordBatchStream,
    file_column: Arc<String>,
    survivors: BarrierSurvivorSet,
    map: HashMap<String, usize>,
    file_partitions: Vec<MergeBarrierPartition>,
}

impl MergeBarrierStream {
    pub fn new(
        input: SendableRecordBatchStream,
        schema: SchemaRef,
        survivors: BarrierSurvivorSet,
        file_column: Arc<String>,
    ) -> Self {
        // Always allocate for a null bucket at index 0;
        let file_partitions = vec![MergeBarrierPartition::new(None)];

        MergeBarrierStream {
            schema,
            state: State::Feed,
            input,
            file_column,
            survivors,
            file_partitions,
            map: HashMap::new(),
        }
    }
}

fn get_count(batch: &RecordBatch, column: &str) -> DataFusionResult<usize> {
    batch
        .column_by_name(column)
        .map(|array| array.null_count())
        .ok_or_else(|| {
            DataFusionError::External(Box::new(DeltaTableError::Generic(
                "Required operation column is missing".to_string(),
            )))
        })
}

impl Stream for MergeBarrierStream {
    type Item = DataFusionResult<RecordBatch>;

    fn poll_next(mut self: Pin<&mut Self>, cx: &mut Context<'_>) -> Poll<Option<Self::Item>> {
        loop {
            match self.state {
                State::Feed => {
                    match self.input.poll_next_unpin(cx) {
                        Poll::Ready(Some(Ok(batch))) => {
                            let file_dictionary = get_path_column(&batch, &self.file_column)?;

                            // For each record batch, the key for a file path is not stable.
                            // We can iterate through the dictionary and lookup the correspond string for each record and then lookup the correct `file_partition` for that value.
                            // However this approach exposes the cost of hashing so we want to minimize that as much as possible.
                            // A map from an arrow dictionary key to the correct index of `file_partition` is created for each batch that's processed.
                            // This ensures we only need to hash each file path at most once per batch.
                            let mut key_map = Vec::with_capacity(file_dictionary.len());

                            for file_name in file_dictionary.values().into_iter() {
                                let key = match file_name {
                                    Some(name) => {



2026-06-01 10:12:28,927 - INFO - swea-agent-delta-io__delta-rs-4333 - ========================= STEP 10 =========================
2026-06-01 10:12:28,930 - DEBUG - swea-lm-delta-io__delta-rs-4333 - n_cache_control: 2
2026-06-01 10:12:31,331 - DEBUG - swea-lm-delta-io__delta-rs-4333 - Response: ModelResponse(id='chatcmpl-DltvBtXGgntp6w1Nl4xa8wN6Q6zGx', created=1780308749, model='gpt-5.5-2026-04-24', object='chat.completion', system_fingerprint=None, choices=[Choices(finish_reason='tool_calls', index=0, message=Message(content=None, role='assistant', tool_calls=[ChatCompletionMessageToolCall(function=Function(arguments='{"command":"sed -n \'260,560p\' /testbed/crates/core/src/operations/merge/barrier.rs"}', name='bash'), id='call_5M11XaHGWspJOEjFtkHywPSR', type='function')], function_call=None, provider_specific_fields={'refusal': None}, annotations=[]), provider_specific_fields={'content_filter_results': {}})], usage=Usage(completion_tokens=40, prompt_tokens=20571, total_tokens=20611, completion_tokens_details=CompletionTokensDetailsWrapper(accepted_prediction_tokens=0, audio_tokens=0, reasoning_tokens=0, rejected_prediction_tokens=0, text_tokens=None, image_tokens=None, video_tokens=None), prompt_tokens_details=PromptTokensDetailsWrapper(audio_tokens=0, cached_tokens=16000, text_tokens=None, image_tokens=None, video_tokens=None), latency_checkpoint={'engine_tbt_ms': 6, 'engine_ttft_ms': 445, 'engine_ttlt_ms': 693, 'pre_inference_ms': 233, 'service_tbt_ms': 6, 'service_ttft_ms': 951, 'service_ttlt_ms': 1197, 'total_duration_ms': 976, 'user_visible_ttft_ms': 719}), service_tier='default', prompt_filter_results=[{'prompt_index': 0, 'content_filter_results': {}}])

2026-06-01 10:12:31,644 - DEBUG - swea-tools-delta-io__delta-rs-4333 - Retrieved state from environment: {'working_dir': '/testbed'}
2026-06-01 10:12:31,646 - INFO - swea-agent-delta-io__delta-rs-4333 - 🤖 MODEL INPUT
OBSERVATION:

                                    Some(name) => {
                                        if !self.map.contains_key(name) {
                                            let key = self.file_partitions.len();
                                            let part_stream =
                                                MergeBarrierPartition::new(Some(name.to_string()));
                                            self.file_partitions.push(part_stream);
                                            self.map.insert(name.to_string(), key);
                                        }
                                        // Safe unwrap due to the above
                                        *self.map.get(name).unwrap()
                                    }
                                    None => 0,
                                };
                                key_map.push(key)
                            }

                            let mut indices: Vec<_> =
                                Vec::with_capacity(self.file_partitions.len());
                            for _ in 0..self.file_partitions.len() {
                                indices.push(UInt64Builder::with_capacity(batch.num_rows()));
                            }

                            for (idx, key) in file_dictionary.keys().iter().enumerate() {
                                match key {
                                    Some(value) => {
                                        indices[key_map[value as usize]].append_value(idx as u64)
                                    }
                                    None => indices[0].append_value(idx as u64),
                                }
                            }

                            let batches: Vec<Result<(usize, RecordBatch), DataFusionError>> =
                                indices
                                    .into_iter()
                                    .enumerate()
                                    .filter_map(|(partition, mut indices)| {
                                        let indices = indices.finish();
                                        (!indices.is_empty()).then_some((partition, indices))
                                    })
                                    .map(move |(partition, indices)| {
                                        // Produce batches based on indices
                                        let columns = batch
                                            .columns()
                                            .iter()
                                            .map(|c| {
                                                Ok(arrow::compute::take(
                                                    c.as_ref(),
                                                    &indices,
                                                    None,
                                                )?)
                                            })
                                            .collect::<DataFusionResult<Vec<ArrayRef>>>()?;

                                        // This unwrap is safe since the processed batched has the same schema
                                        let batch =
                                            RecordBatch::try_new(batch.schema(), columns).unwrap();

                                        Ok((partition, batch))
                                    })
                                    .collect();

                            for batch in batches {
                                match batch {
                                    Ok((partition, batch)) => {
                                        self.file_partitions[partition].feed(batch)?;
                                    }
                                    Err(err) => {
                                        self.state = State::Abort;
                                        return Poll::Ready(Some(Err(err)));
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                            self.state = State::Drain;
                            continue;
                        }
                        Poll::Ready(Some(Err(err))) => {
                            self.state = State::Abort;
                            return Poll::Ready(Some(Err(err)));
                        }
                        Poll::Ready(None) => {
                            self.state = State::Finalize;
                            continue;
                        }
                        Poll::Pending => return Poll::Pending,
                    }
                }
                State::Drain => {
                    for part in &mut self.file_partitions {
                        if let Some(batch) = part.drain() {
                            return Poll::Ready(Some(Ok(batch)));
                        }
                    }

                    self.state = State::Feed;
                    continue;
                }
                State::Finalize => {
                    for part in &mut self.file_partitions {
                        if let Some(batch) = part.drain() {
                            return Poll::Ready(Some(Ok(batch)));
                        }
                    }

                    {
                        for part in &self.file_partitions {
                            match part.state {
                                PartitionBarrierState::Closed => {}
                                PartitionBarrierState::Open => {
                                    if let Some(file_name) = &part.file_name {
                                        self.survivors.insert(file_name.to_owned());
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    self.state = State::Done;
                    continue;
                }
                State::Abort => return Poll::Ready(None),
                State::Done => return Poll::Ready(None),
            }
        }
    }

    fn size_hint(&self) -> (usize, Option<usize>) {
        (0, self.input.size_hint().1)
    }
}

impl RecordBatchStream for MergeBarrierStream {
    fn schema(&self) -> SchemaRef {
        self.schema.clone()
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Hash, Eq, PartialEq, PartialOrd)]
pub(crate) struct MergeBarrier {
    pub input: LogicalPlan,
    pub expr: Expr,
    pub file_column: Arc<String>,
}

impl UserDefinedLogicalNodeCore for MergeBarrier {
    fn name(&self) -> &str {
        "MergeBarrier"
    }

    fn inputs(&self) -> Vec<&datafusion::logical_expr::LogicalPlan> {
        vec![&self.input]
    }

    fn schema(&self) -> &datafusion::common::DFSchemaRef {
        self.input.schema()
    }

    fn expressions(&self) -> Vec<datafusion::logical_expr::Expr> {
        vec![self.expr.clone()]
    }

    fn fmt_for_explain(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter) -> std::fmt::Result {
        write!(f, "MergeBarrier")
    }

    fn with_exprs_and_inputs(
        &self,
        exprs: Vec<datafusion::logical_expr::Expr>,
        inputs: Vec<datafusion::logical_expr::LogicalPlan>,
    ) -> DataFusionResult<Self> {
        Ok(MergeBarrier {
            input: inputs[0].clone(),
            file_column: self.file_column.clone(),
            expr: exprs[0].clone(),
        })
    }
}

pub(crate) fn find_node<T: 'static>(
    parent: &Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>,
) -> Option<Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>> {
    //! Used to locate a Node::<T> after the planner converts the logical node
    if parent.as_any().downcast_ref::<T>().is_some() {
        return Some(parent.to_owned());
    }

    for child in &parent.children() {
        let res = find_node::<T>(child);
        if res.is_some() {
            return res;
        }
    }

    None
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::BarrierSurvivorSet;
    use crate::operations::merge::MergeBarrierExec;
    use crate::operations::merge::{
        TARGET_DELETE_COLUMN, TARGET_INSERT_COLUMN, TARGET_UPDATE_COLUMN,
    };
    use arrow::datatypes::Schema as ArrowSchema;
    use arrow_array::RecordBatch;
    use arrow_array::StringArray;
    use arrow_array::{DictionaryArray, UInt16Array};
    use arrow_schema::DataType as ArrowDataType;
    use arrow_schema::Field;
    use datafusion::assert_batches_sorted_eq;
    use datafusion::datasource::memory::MemorySourceConfig;
    use datafusion::execution::TaskContext;
    use datafusion::physical_expr::expressions::Column;
    use datafusion::physical_plan::ExecutionPlan;
    use datafusion::physical_plan::coalesce_batches::CoalesceBatchesExec;
    use futures::StreamExt;
    use std::sync::Arc;

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_barrier() {
        // Validate that files without modifications are dropped and that files with changes passthrough
        // File 0: No Changes
        // File 1: Contains an update
        // File 2: Contains a delete
        // null (id: 3): is a insert

        let schema = get_schema();
        let keys = UInt16Array::from(vec![Some(0), Some(1), Some(2), None]);
        let values = StringArray::from(vec![Some("file0"), Some("file1"), Some("file2")]);
        let dict = DictionaryArray::new(keys, Arc::new(values));

        let batch = RecordBatch::try_new(
            schema.clone(),
            vec![
                Arc::new(arrow::array::StringArray::from(vec!["0", "1", "2", "3"])),
                Arc::new(dict),
                //insert column
                Arc::new(arrow::array::BooleanArray::from(vec![
                    Some(false),
                    Some(false),
                    Some(false),
                    None,
                ])),
                //update column
                Arc::new(arrow::array::BooleanArray::from(vec![
                    Some(false),
                    None,
                    Some(false),
                    Some(false),
                ])),
                //delete column
                Arc::new(arrow::array::BooleanArray::from(vec![
                    Some(false),
                    Some(false),
                    None,
                    Some(false),
                ])),
            ],
        )
        .unwrap();

        let (actual, survivors) = execute(vec![batch]).await;
        let expected = vec![
            "+----+-----------------+--------------------------+--------------------------+--------------------------+",
            "| id | __delta_rs_path | __delta_rs_target_insert | __delta_rs_target_update | __delta_rs_target_delete |",
            "+----+-----------------+--------------------------+--------------------------+--------------------------+",
            "| 1  | file1           | false                    |                          | false                    |",
            "| 2  | file2           | false                    | false                    |                          |",
            "| 3  |                 |                          | false                    | false                    |",
            "+----+-----------------+--------------------------+--------------------------+--------------------------+",
        ];
        assert_batches_sorted_eq!(&expected, &actual);

        assert!(!survivors.contains(&"file0".to_string()));
        assert!(survivors.contains(&"file1".to_string()));
        assert!(survivors.contains(&"file2".to_string()));
        assert_eq!(survivors.len(), 2);
    }

   233	    /// The physical arrow schema exposed by the table provider
   234	    ///
   235	    /// This includes any adjustments to the logical schema
   236	    /// such as dictionary encoding of partition columns or
   237	    /// view types.
   238	    pub(crate) fn table_schema(&self, table_config: &TableConfiguration) -> Result<SchemaRef> {
   239	        let table_schema: Schema = table_config.schema().as_ref().try_into_arrow()?;
   240	        self.physical_arrow_schema(table_config, &table_schema)
   241	    }
   242	
   243	    fn physical_arrow_schema(
   244	        &self,
   245	        table_config: &TableConfiguration,
   246	        base: &Schema,
   247	    ) -> Result<SchemaRef> {
   248	        // delta exposes a logical schema which gets converted to default physical types,
   249	        // but we may want specific physical types
   250	        // (e.g. dictionary encoded partition columns, view types, etc) so we transform
   251	        // the schema accordingly here
   252	        let cols = table_config.metadata().partition_columns();
   253	        let table_schema = Arc::new(Schema::new(
   254	            base.fields()
   255	                .iter()
   256	                .map(|f| self.map_field(f.clone(), cols))
   257	                .collect_vec(),
   258	        ));
   259	        Ok(table_schema)
   260	    }

    40	#[derive(Debug, PartialEq)]
    41	pub(crate) struct DvMaskResult {
    42	    pub selection: Option<Vec<bool>>,
    43	    pub should_remove: bool,
    44	}
    45	
    46	/// Consume the per-file deletion-vector keep-mask for the current batch.
    47	///
    48	/// The keep-mask is stored once per file and consumed incrementally as parquet
    49	/// batches are produced:
    50	/// - If the mask is shorter than the batch, missing trailing entries are
    51	///   treated as `true` (keep row).
    52	/// - If the mask is longer than the batch, the remainder is preserved for the
    53	///   next batch from the same file.
    54	///
    55	/// This function intentionally does not error when `selection_vector.len()` is
    56	/// greater than `batch_num_rows`; that is expected when one file spans multiple
    57	/// input batches.
    58	pub(crate) fn consume_dv_mask(
    59	    selection_vector: &mut Vec<bool>,
    60	    batch_num_rows: usize,
    61	) -> DvMaskResult {
    62	    if selection_vector.is_empty() {
    63	        return DvMaskResult {
    64	            selection: None,
    65	            should_remove: true,
    66	        };
    67	    }
    68	
    69	    if selection_vector.len() >= batch_num_rows {
    70	        let sv: Vec<bool> = selection_vector.drain(0..batch_num_rows).collect();
    71	        let is_empty = selection_vector.is_empty();
    72	        DvMaskResult {
    73	            selection: Some(sv),
    74	            should_remove: is_empty,
    75	        }
    76	    } else {
    77	        let mut sv: Vec<bool> = std::mem::take(selection_vector);
    78	        sv.resize(batch_num_rows, true);
    79	        DvMaskResult {
    80	            selection: Some(sv),
    81	            should_remove: true,
    82	        }
    83	    }
    84	}
    85	
    86	/// Physical execution plan for scanning Delta tables.
    87	///
    88	/// Wraps a Parquet reader execution plan and applies Delta Lake protocol transformations
    89	/// to produce the logical table data. This includes:
    90	///
    91	/// - **Column mapping**: Translates physical column names to logical names
    92	/// - **Partition values**: Materializes partition column values from file paths
    93	/// - **Deletion vectors**: Filters out deleted rows using per-file selection vectors
    94	/// - **Schema evolution**: Handles missing columns and type coercion
    95	///
    96	/// # Data Flow
    97	///
    98	/// 1. Inner [`input`](Self::input) plan reads raw Parquet data
    99	/// 2. Per-file [`transforms`](Self::transforms) convert physical to logical schema
   100	/// 3. [`selection_vectors`](Self::selection_vectors) filter deleted rows
   101	/// 4. Result is cast to [`result_schema`](KernelScanPlan::result_schema)
   102	#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
   103	pub struct DeltaScanExec {
   104	    scan_plan: Arc<KernelScanPlan>,
   105	    /// Execution plan yielding the raw data read from data files.
   106	    input: Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>,
   107	    /// Transforms to be applied to data eminating from individual files
   108	    transforms: Arc<HashMap<String, ExpressionRef>>,
   109	    /// Selection vectors to be applied to data read from individual files
   110	    selection_vectors: Arc<DashMap<String, Vec<bool>>>,
   111	    /// Execution metrics
   112	    metrics: ExecutionPlanMetricsSet,
   113	    /// Column name for the file id
   114	    file_id_column: String,
   115	    /// plan properties
   116	    properties: PlanProperties,
   117	    /// Denotes if file ids should be returned as part of the output
   118	    retain_file_ids: bool,
   119	    /// Aggregated partition column statistics
   120	    partition_stats: HashMap<String, ColumnStatistics>,

   382	        // Clone the metric so the timer guard does not immutably borrow `self`,
   383	        // which would conflict with the `&mut self` calls below.
   384	        let elapsed = self.baseline_metrics.elapsed_compute().clone();

    18	async fn create_table(table_uri: &str, partition: Option<Vec<&str>>) -> DeltaTable {
    19	    let table_schema = get_delta_schema();
    20	    let table_url = url::Url::from_directory_path(table_uri).unwrap();

    23	        .create()
    24	        .with_columns(table_schema.fields().cloned())

    26	        .await
    27	        .expect("Failed to create table");
    28

    30	    write_data(table, &schema).await
    31	}

    64	        Arc::clone(schema),
    65	        vec![
    66	            Arc::new(arrow::array::StringArray::from(vec!["A", "B", "C", "D"])),
    67	            Arc::new(arrow::array::Int32Array::from(vec![1, 10, 10, 100])),
    68	            Arc::new(arrow::array::StringArray::from(vec![
    69	                "2021-02-01",
    70	                "2021-02-01",
    71	                "2021-02-02",
    72	                "2021-02-02",
    73	            ])),
    74	        ],
    75	    )
    76	    .unwrap();
    77	    // write some data
    78	    table
    79	        .write(vec![batch.clone()])
    80	        .with_save_mode(SaveMode::Append)
    81	        .await
    82	        .unwrap()
    83	}
    84	
    85	fn create_test_data() -> (DataFrame, DataFrame) {
    86	    let schema = get_arrow_schema();
    87	    let ctx = SessionContext::new();
    88	    let batch = RecordBatch::try_new(
    89	        Arc::clone(&schema),
    90	        vec![
    91	            Arc::new(arrow::array::StringArray::from(vec!["C", "D"])),
    92	            Arc::new(arrow::array::Int32Array::from(vec![10, 20])),
    93	            Arc::new(arrow::array::StringArray::from(vec![
    94	                "2021-02-02",
    95	                "2021-02-02",
    96	            ])),
    97	        ],
    98	    )
    99	    .unwrap();
   100	    let df1 = ctx.read_batch(batch).unwrap();
   101	    let batch = RecordBatch::try_new(
   102	        Arc::clone(&schema),
   103	        vec![
   104	            Arc::new(arrow::array::StringArray::from(vec!["E", "F"])),
   105	            Arc::new(arrow::array::Int32Array::from(vec![10, 20])),
   106	            Arc::new(arrow::array::StringArray::from(vec![
   107	                "2021-02-03",
   108	                "2021-02-03",
   109	            ])),
   110	        ],
   111	    )
   112	    .unwrap();
   113	    let df2 = ctx.read_batch(batch).unwrap();
   114	    (df1, df2)
   115	}
   116	
   117	async fn merge(
   118	    table: DeltaTable,
   119	    df: DataFrame,
   120	    predicate: Expr,
   121	) -> DeltaResult<(DeltaTable, MergeMetrics)> {
   122	    table
   123	        .merge(df, predicate)
   124	        .with_source_alias("source")
   125	        .with_target_alias("target")
   126	        .when_matched_update(|update| {
   127	            update
   128	                .update("value", col("source.value"))
   129	                .update("event_date", col("source.event_date"))
   130	        })
   131	        .unwrap()
   132	        .when_not_matched_insert(|insert| {
   133	            insert
   134	                .set("id", col("source.id"))
   135	                .set("value", col("source.value"))
   136	                .set("event_date", col("source.event_date"))
   137	        })
   138	        .unwrap()
   139	        .await
   140	}
   141	
   142	#[tokio::test]
   143	async fn test_merge_concurrent_conflict() {
   144	    // Overlapping id ranges -> Commit conflict
   145	    let tmp_dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();
   146	    let table_uri = tmp_dir.path().to_str().to_owned().unwrap();
   147	
   148	    let table_ref1 = create_table(table_uri, Some(vec!["event_date"])).await;
   149	    let table_url = Url::from_directory_path(table_uri).unwrap();
   150	    let table_ref2 = open_table(table_url).await.unwrap();
   151	    let (df1, _df2) = create_test_data();
   152	
   153	    let expr = col("target.id").eq(col("source.id"));
   154	    let (_table_ref1, _metrics) = merge(table_ref1, df1.clone(), expr.clone()).await.unwrap();
   155	    let result = merge(table_ref2, df1, expr).await;
   156	
   157	    assert!(matches!(
   158	        result.as_ref().unwrap_err(),
   159	        DeltaTableError::Transaction { .. }
   160	    ));
   161	    if let DeltaTableError::Transaction { source } = result.unwrap_err() {
   162	        assert!(matches!(source, TransactionError::CommitConflict(_)));
   163	    }
   164	}
   165	
   166	#[tokio::test]
   167	async fn test_merge_different_range() {
   168	    // No overlapping id ranges -> No conflict
   169	    let tmp_dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();
   170	    let table_uri = tmp_dir.path().to_str().to_owned().unwrap();
   171	
   172	    let table_ref1 = create_table(table_uri, Some(vec!["event_date"])).await;

   174	    let table_ref2 = open_table(table_url).await.unwrap();
   175	    let (df1, df2) = create_test_data();
   176	
   177	    let expr = col("target.id").eq(col("source.id"));
   178	    let (_table_ref1, _metrics) = merge(table_ref1, df1, expr.clone()).await.unwrap();
   179	    let result = merge(table_ref2, df2, expr).await;
   180

   437	async fn get_read_plan(
   438	    state: &dyn Session,
   439	    files_by_store: impl IntoIterator<Item = FilesByStore>,
   440	    // Schema of physical file columns to read from Parquet (no Delta partitions, no file-id).
   441	    //
   442	    // This is also the schema used for Parquet pruning/pushdown. It may include view types
   443	    // (e.g. Utf8View/BinaryView) depending on `DeltaScanConfig`.
   444	    parquet_read_schema: &SchemaRef,
   445	    limit: Option<usize>,
   446	    file_id_field: &FieldRef,
   447	    predicate: Option<&Expr>,
   448	) -> Result<Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>> {
   449	    let mut plans = Vec::new();
   450	
   451	    let pq_options = TableParquetOptions {
   452	        global: state.config().options().execution.parquet.clone(),
   453	        ..Default::default()
   454	    };
   455	
   456	    let mut full_read_schema = SchemaBuilder::from(parquet_read_schema.as_ref().clone());
   457	    full_read_schema.push(file_id_field.as_ref().clone().with_nullable(true));
   458	    let full_read_schema = Arc::new(full_read_schema.finish());
   459	    let full_read_df_schema = full_read_schema.clone().to_dfschema()?;
   460	
   461	    for (store_url, files) in files_by_store.into_iter() {
   462	        let reader_factory = Arc::new(CachedParquetFileReaderFactory::new(
   463	            state.runtime_env().object_store(&store_url)?,
   464	            state.runtime_env().cache_manager.get_file_metadata_cache(),
   465	        ));
   466	
   467	        // NOTE: In the "next" provider, DataFusion's Parquet scan partition fields are file-id
   468	        // only. Delta partition columns/values are injected via kernel transforms and handled
   469	        // above Parquet, so they are not part of the Parquet partition schema here.
   470	        let table_schema =
   471	            TableSchema::new(parquet_read_schema.clone(), vec![file_id_field.clone()]);
   472	        let full_table_schema = table_schema.table_schema().clone();
   473	        let mut file_source = ParquetSource::new(table_schema)
   474	            .with_table_parquet_options(pq_options.clone())
   475	            .with_parquet_file_reader_factory(reader_factory);
   476	
   477	        // TODO(roeap); we might be able to also push selection vectors into the read plan
   478	        // by creating parquet access plans. However we need to make sure this does not
   479	        // interfere with other delta features like row ids.
   480	        let has_selection_vectors = files.iter().any(|(_, sv)| sv.is_some());
   481	        if !has_selection_vectors && let Some(pred) = predicate {
   482	            // Predicate pushdown can reference the synthetic file-id partition column.
   483	            // Use the full read schema (data columns + file-id) when planning.
   484	            let physical = state.create_physical_expr(pred.clone(), &full_read_df_schema)?;
   485	            file_source = file_source
   486	                .with_predicate(physical)
   487	                .with_pushdown_filters(true);
   488	        }

///     .build()?;
///
/// // Create a window expression for percent rank partitioned on column a
/// // equivalent to:
/// // `PERCENT_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY a ORDER BY b ASC NULLS LAST IGNORE NULLS)`
/// // percent_rank is an udwf function in another crate
/// # fn percent_rank() -> Expr {
/// unimplemented!() }
/// let window = percent_rank()
///     .partition_by(vec![col("a")])
///     .order_by(vec![col("b").sort(true, true)])
///     .null_treatment(NullTreatment::IgnoreNulls)
///     .build()?;
/// #     Ok(())
/// # }
/// ```
pub trait ExprFunctionExt {
    /// Add `ORDER BY <order_by>`
    fn order_by(self, order_by: Vec<Sort>) -> ExprFuncBuilder;
    /// Add `FILTER <filter>`
    fn filter(self, filter: Expr) -> ExprFuncBuilder;
    /// Add `DISTINCT`
    fn distinct(self) -> ExprFuncBuilder;
    /// Add `RESPECT NULLS` or `IGNORE NULLS`
    fn null_treatment(
        self,
        null_treatment: impl Into<Option<NullTreatment>>,
    ) -> ExprFuncBuilder;
    /// Add `PARTITION BY`
    fn partition_by(self, partition_by: Vec<Expr>) -> ExprFuncBuilder;
    /// Add appropriate window frame conditions
    fn window_frame(self, window_frame: WindowFrame) -> ExprFuncBuilder;
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub enum ExprFuncKind {
    Aggregate(AggregateFunction),
    Window(Box<WindowFunction>),
}

/// Implementation of [`ExprFunctionExt`].
///
/// See [`ExprFunctionExt`] for usage and examples
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ExprFuncBuilder {
    fun: Option<ExprFuncKind>,
    order_by: Option<Vec<Sort>>,
    filter: Option<Expr>,
    distinct: bool,
    null_treatment: Option<NullTreatment>,
    partition_by: Option<Vec<Expr>>,
    window_frame: Option<WindowFrame>,
}

impl ExprFuncBuilder {
    /// Create a new `ExprFuncBuilder`, see [`ExprFunctionExt`]
    fn new(fun: Option<ExprFuncKind>) -> Self {
        Self {
            fun,
            order_by: None,
            filter: None,
            distinct: false,
            null_treatment: None,
            partition_by: None,
            window_frame: None,
        }
    }

    /// Updates and returns the in progress [`Expr::AggregateFunction`] or [`Expr::WindowFunction`]
    ///
    /// # Errors:
pub struct WindowFunction {
    /// Name of the function
    pub fun: WindowFunctionDefinition,
    pub params: WindowFunctionParams,
}

#[derive(Clone, PartialEq, Eq, PartialOrd, Hash, Debug)]
pub struct WindowFunctionParams {
    /// List of expressions to feed to the functions as arguments
    pub args: Vec<Expr>,
    /// List of partition by expressions
    pub partition_by: Vec<Expr>,
    /// List of order by expressions
    pub order_by: Vec<Sort>,
    /// Window frame
    pub window_frame: WindowFrame,
    /// Optional filter expression (FILTER (WHERE ...))
    pub filter: Option<Box<Expr>>,
    /// Specifies how NULL value is treated: ignore or respect
    pub null_treatment: Option<NullTreatment>,
    /// Distinct flag
    pub distinct: bool,
}

impl WindowFunction {
    /// Create a new Window expression with the specified argument an
    /// empty `OVER` clause
    pub fn new(fun: impl Into<WindowFunctionDefinition>, args: Vec<Expr>) -> Self {
        Self {
            fun: fun.into(),
            params: WindowFunctionParams {
                args,
                partition_by: Vec::default(),
                order_by: Vec::default(),
                window_frame: WindowFrame::new(None),
                filter: None,
                null_treatment: None,
                distinct: false,
            },
        }
    }
